{Effects Callbacks}
	function store_FX_data

		%fx_data[($cur_tile * 13) + $fx_pointer] := get_control_par(%effects_control_id[$fx_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
	end function
		
	on ui_control ($trans_attack_sld)
		set_control_par(%stat_fx_lbl_id[00], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, 16)
		$bus_index := $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$cur_tile]
		set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_TR_ATTACK,$trans_attack_sld,-1,$TRANS1_SLOT,$bus_index)
		$fx_pointer := $TRANS_ATTACK
		call store_FX_data
		set_control_par_str (%effects_control_id[$TRANS_ATTACK],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,...
                      get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_TR_ATTACK,-1,$TRANS1_SLOT,$bus_index) & " %")
		set_text ($lbl_trans_attack,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_TR_ATTACK,-1,$TRANS1_SLOT,$bus_index) & " %")
		%lbl_fx_last_time[$TRANS_ATTACK] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
		wait($LABEL_WAIT * 1000)
		if($ENGINE_UPTIME - %lbl_fx_last_time[$TRANS_ATTACK] > $LABEL_WAIT - 5)
			set_text ($lbl_trans_attack,"")
			set_control_par(%stat_fx_lbl_id[00], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, 0)
		end if
	end on
	on ui_control ($trans_sustain_sld)
	set_control_par(%stat_fx_lbl_id[01], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, 16)
		$bus_index := $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$cur_tile]
		set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_TR_SUSTAIN,$trans_sustain_sld,-1,$TRANS1_SLOT,$bus_index)
		$fx_pointer := $TRANS_RELEASE
		call store_FX_data
		set_control_par_str (%lbl_fx_id[$TRANS_RELEASE],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,...
                      get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_TR_SUSTAIN,-1,$TRANS1_SLOT,$bus_index) & " %")
		set_text ($lbl_trans_sustain,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_TR_SUSTAIN,-1,$TRANS1_SLOT,$bus_index) & " %")
		%lbl_fx_last_time[$TRANS_RELEASE] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
		wait($LABEL_WAIT * 1000)
		if($ENGINE_UPTIME - %lbl_fx_last_time[$TRANS_RELEASE] > $LABEL_WAIT - 5)
			set_text ($lbl_trans_sustain,"")
			set_control_par(%stat_fx_lbl_id[01], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, 0)
		end if
	end on
	
	{Feedback Compressor}
	on ui_control ($comp_amount_sld)
		set_control_par(%stat_fx_lbl_id[02], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, 16)
		$bus_index := $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$cur_tile]
		set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_FCOMP_INPUT,  %ingain[$comp_amount_sld],  -1, $COMP_SLOT,$bus_index)
		set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_FCOMP_MAKEUP, %outgain[$comp_amount_sld], -1 ,$COMP_SLOT,$bus_index)
		$fx_pointer := $COMP_AMOUNT
		call store_FX_data
		set_control_par_str (%lbl_fx_id[$COMP_AMOUNT],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, 79*($comp_amount_sld*100/100)/100 & " %")
		set_text ($lbl_comp_amount, 79*($comp_amount_sld*100/100)/100 & " %")
		%lbl_fx_last_time[$COMP_AMOUNT] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
		wait($LABEL_WAIT * 1000)
		if($ENGINE_UPTIME - %lbl_fx_last_time[$COMP_AMOUNT] > $LABEL_WAIT - 5)
			set_text ($lbl_comp_amount,"")
			set_control_par(%stat_fx_lbl_id[02], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, 0)
		end if
	end on
	on ui_control ($comp_attack_sld)
		set_control_par(%stat_fx_lbl_id[03], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, 16)
		$bus_index := $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$cur_tile]
		set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_FCOMP_ATTACK, $comp_attack_sld,  -1, $COMP_SLOT,$bus_index)
		$fx_pointer := $COMP_ATTACK
		call store_FX_data
		set_control_par_str (%lbl_fx_id[$COMP_ATTACK],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,...
                      get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_FCOMP_ATTACK,-1,$COMP_SLOT,$bus_index) & " ms")
		set_text ($lbl_comp_attack,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_FCOMP_ATTACK,-1,$COMP_SLOT,$bus_index) & " ms")
		%lbl_fx_last_time[$TRANS_ATTACK] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
		wait($LABEL_WAIT * 1000)
		if($ENGINE_UPTIME - %lbl_fx_last_time[$COMP_ATTACK] > $LABEL_WAIT - 5)
			set_text ($lbl_comp_attack,"")
			set_control_par(%stat_fx_lbl_id[03], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, 0)
		end if
	end on
	on ui_control ($sat_gain_sld)

		end if
	end on
	on ui_control ($sat_level_sld)

                      get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,-1,$SAT_SLOT,$bus_index) & " dB")

		%lbl_fx_last_time[$SAT_LEVEL] := $ENGINE_UPTIME

	on ui_control ($eq_lf_freq_sld)

                      get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_LF_FREQ,-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index) & " Hz")
		set_text ($lbl_eq_lf_freq,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_LF_FREQ,-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index) & " Hz")

		$bus_index := $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$cur_tile]
		set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_HF_GAIN,$eq_hf_db_sld,-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index)
		$fx_pointer := $EQ_HI_GAIN

		set_control_par_str (%lbl_fx_id[$EQ_HI_GAIN],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,...
                      get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_HF_GAIN,-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index) & " dB")

		%lbl_fx_last_time[$EQ_HI_GAIN] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
		wait($LABEL_WAIT * 1000)
		if($ENGINE_UPTIME - %lbl_fx_last_time[$EQ_HI_GAIN] > $LABEL_WAIT - 5)
			set_text ($lbl_eq_hf_db,"")
			set_control_par(%stat_fx_lbl_id[11], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, 0)
		end if
	end on
	on ui_control ($reverb_send_sld)
		set_control_par(%stat_fx_lbl_id[12], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, 16)
		$bus_index := $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$cur_tile]

		$send_value := $reverb_send_sld

		if($send_value < 500)
			$send_value := $send_value * 1260
		else
			if($send_value = 500)
				$send_value := 630000
			else
				$send_value := 630000 + (328*($send_value - 500))
			end if
		end if

		set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SENDLEVEL_0,$send_value,-1,$SEND_SLOT,$bus_index)
		$fx_pointer := $RVB_SEND
		call store_FX_data
		set_control_par_str (%effects_control_id[$RVB_SEND],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,...
                      get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SENDLEVEL_0,-1,$SEND_SLOT,$bus_index) & " dB")
		set_text ($lbl_reverb_send,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SENDLEVEL_0,-1,$SEND_SLOT,$bus_index) & " dB")
		%lbl_fx_last_time[$RVB_SEND] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
		wait($LABEL_WAIT * 1000)
		if($ENGINE_UPTIME - %lbl_fx_last_time[$RVB_SEND] > $LABEL_WAIT - 5)
			set_text ($lbl_reverb_send,"")
			set_control_par(%stat_fx_lbl_id[12], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, 0)
		end if
	end on

	on ui_control($onoff_trans)
		$bus_index := $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$cur_tile]
		%onoff_data[($cur_tile * 4) + 0] := $onoff_trans
		set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_EFFECT_BYPASS,($onoff_trans+1) mod 2,-1,$TRANS1_SLOT,$bus_index)
	end on
	on ui_control($onoff_comp)
		$bus_index := $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$cur_tile]
		%onoff_data[($cur_tile * 4) + 1] := $onoff_comp
		set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_EFFECT_BYPASS,($onoff_comp+1) mod 2,-1,$COMP_SLOT,$bus_index)
	end on
	on ui_control($onoff_sat)
		$bus_index := $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$cur_tile]
		%onoff_data[($cur_tile * 4) + 2] := $onoff_sat
		set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_EFFECT_BYPASS,($onoff_sat+1) mod 2,-1,$SAT_SLOT,$bus_index)
	end on
	on ui_control($onoff_eq)
		$bus_index := $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$cur_tile]
		%onoff_data[($cur_tile * 4) + 3] := $onoff_eq
		set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_EFFECT_BYPASS,($onoff_eq+1) mod 2,-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index)
	end on

{MASTER Effects Callbacks}
	function store_master_FX_data

		%master_fx_data[$fx_pointer] := get_control_par(%mast_effects_control_id[$fx_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
	end function
		
	on ui_control ($mast_trans_attack_sld)
		set_control_par(%stat_mast_lbl_fx_id[00], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE,16)
		$bus_index := 1
		set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_TR_ATTACK,$mast_trans_attack_sld,-1,$TRANS1_SLOT,$bus_index)
		$fx_pointer := $MAST_TRANS_ATTACK
		call store_master_FX_data
		set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$fx_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,...
                      get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_TR_ATTACK,-1,$TRANS1_SLOT,$bus_index) & " %")
		set_text ($lbl_mast_trans_attack,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_TR_ATTACK,-1,$TRANS1_SLOT,$bus_index) & " %")
		%lbl_mast_fx_last_time[$MAST_TRANS_ATTACK] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
		wait($LABEL_WAIT * 1000)
		if($ENGINE_UPTIME - %lbl_mast_fx_last_time[$MAST_TRANS_ATTACK] > $LABEL_WAIT - 5)
			set_text ($lbl_mast_trans_attack,"")
			if ($cur_tile = $TILE_MASTER)
				set_control_par(%stat_mast_lbl_fx_id[00], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE,0)
			end if
		end if
	end on
	on ui_control ($mast_trans_sustain_sld)
		set_control_par(%stat_mast_lbl_fx_id[01], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE,16)
		$bus_index := 1
		set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_TR_SUSTAIN,$mast_trans_sustain_sld,-1,$TRANS1_SLOT,$bus_index)
		$fx_pointer := $MAST_TRANS_RELEASE
		call store_master_FX_data
		set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$fx_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,...
                      get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_TR_SUSTAIN,-1,$TRANS1_SLOT,$bus_index) & " %")
		set_text ($lbl_mast_trans_sustain,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_TR_SUSTAIN,-1,$TRANS1_SLOT,$bus_index) & " %")
		%lbl_mast_fx_last_time[$MAST_TRANS_RELEASE] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
		wait($LABEL_WAIT * 1000)
		if($ENGINE_UPTIME - %lbl_mast_fx_last_time[$MAST_TRANS_RELEASE] > $LABEL_WAIT - 5)
			set_text ($lbl_mast_trans_sustain,"")
			if ($cur_tile = $TILE_MASTER)

			end if
		end if
	end on

		set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$fx_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,...
                      get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SHAPE,-1,$SAT_SLOT,$bus_index) & " %")
		set_text ($lbl_mast_sat_gain,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SHAPE,-1,$SAT_SLOT,$bus_index) & " %")
		%lbl_mast_fx_last_time[$MAST_SAT_GAIN] := $ENGINE_UPTIME

		if($ENGINE_UPTIME - %lbl_mast_fx_last_time[$MAST_SAT_GAIN] > $LABEL_WAIT - 5)
			set_text ($lbl_mast_sat_gain,"")
			if ($cur_tile = $TILE_MASTER)
				set_control_par(%stat_mast_lbl_fx_id[06], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE,0)
			end if
		end if
	end on

{Volume Fader Callbacks}
	function update_vol_bubble_value
		set_control_par($bubble_VOL_id, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, get_control_par(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)*100/71)
		set_control_par($bubble_VOL_id, $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE,$HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
		select ($vol_pointer)
			case $TILE_HIHAT to $TILE_KICK
				set_control_par($bubble_VOL_id, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 45)
				set_control_par($bubble_VOL_id, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y,353 - get_control_par(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)*102/126)
			case $TILE_MASTER
				set_control_par($bubble_VOL_id, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 45)
				set_control_par($bubble_VOL_id, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y,353 - get_control_par(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)*102/126)
			case $TILE_PERC2 to $TILE_TOM3
				set_control_par($bubble_VOL_id, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 45)
				set_control_par($bubble_VOL_id, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y))
			case $TILE_OHS to $TILE_ROOM
				set_control_par($bubble_VOL_id, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 45)
				set_control_par($bubble_VOL_id, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y))
			case $TILE_REV
				set_control_par($bubble_VOL_id, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 45)
				set_control_par($bubble_VOL_id, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y,133 - get_control_par(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)*102/235)
		end select

		%lbl_bubble_VOL_last_time[$vol_pointer] := $ENGINE_UPTIME

		wait($LABEL_WAIT*1000)
		if($ENGINE_UPTIME - %lbl_bubble_VOL_last_time[$vol_pointer] > $LABEL_WAIT - 5)
			set_control_par($bubble_VOL_id, $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE,$HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
		end if
	end function

	function tile_Volume
		{description: sets the volume of the channel/tile}
		{variables = $vol_pointer}
		
		$vol_value := get_control_par(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
		
		if ($vol_pointer = $TILE_REV or $vol_pointer = $TILE_MASTER)
			if ($vol_pointer = $TILE_REV)
				{reverb}
				$vol_value := (%wurzel_zweidrittel[$vol_value]*$cur_volume_verb)/1000
				set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEND_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,$vol_value,-1,$REVERB_SLOT,0)
				set_control_par_str(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SEND_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,-1,$REVERB_SLOT,0) & " dB")
			else
				if ($vol_pointer = $TILE_MASTER)
					{master}
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,(%wurzel_zweidrittel[$vol_value]*$cur_volume)/1000,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,1)
					set_control_par_str(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,1) & " dB")
				end if
			end if
		else
			{channel/kit mic}
			$vol_value := %solo_state[$vol_pointer]*%mute_state[$vol_pointer]*((%wurzel_zweidrittel[$vol_value]*$cur_volume)/1000)
			set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,$vol_value,-1, $SPREAD_SLOT, $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$vol_pointer])
			set_control_par_str(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$vol_pointer]) & " dB")
		end if
	end function

	on ui_control ($vol_KICK)
		$vol_pointer := $TILE_KICK
		call tile_Volume
		call update_vol_bubble_value
	end on
	on ui_control ($vol_SNARE)
		$vol_pointer := $TILE_SNARE
		call tile_Volume
		call update_vol_bubble_value
	end on
	on ui_control ($vol_HIHAT)

		call update_vol_bubble_value
	end on

	end on

	end on

	end on 

{Pan Callbacks}
	function tile_Swap_PAN
		{description: swaps the stereo panorama image and resets the channels}
		
		$a := 0
		while ($a < $NUM_TILES)
			if (%Tile_has_Mixer[$a] > -1 )
				if ($a # $TILE_REV and $a # $TILE_MASTER)
					if ($a = $TILE_OHS or $a = $TILE_OHM or $a = $TILE_ROOM)
						if(%oh_stereo[$a] # -1)
							if(%oh_stereo[$a] = 1)
								{width}
								$pan_value := ($lr_swap + 1) mod 2
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_EFFECT_BYPASS,$pan_value, -1, $BUS_INVERT_SLOT, $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$a])
							else
								{pan}
								$pan_value := 1000000 - get_control_par(%pan_id[$a],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
								set_control_par(%pan_id[$a],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE,$pan_value)
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_STEREO_PAN,$pan_value,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$a])
								set_control_par_str(%pan_id[$a],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_STEREO_PAN,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$a]))
							end if
						end if
					else
						$pan_value := 1000000 - get_control_par(%pan_id[$a],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
						set_control_par(%pan_id[$a],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE,$pan_value)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_STEREO_PAN,$pan_value,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$a])
						set_control_par_str(%pan_id[$a],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_STEREO_PAN,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$a]))
					end if
				end if
			end if
			inc($a)
		end while
	end function

	function update_PAN_bubble_value
		set_control_par($bubble_PAN_id, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, get_control_par(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)/5000)
		set_control_par($bubble_PAN_id, $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE,$HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
		set_control_par($bubble_PAN_id, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 45)
		set_control_par($bubble_PAN_id, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y))
		
		%lbl_bubble_PAN_last_time[$pan_pointer] := $ENGINE_UPTIME

		wait($LABEL_WAIT*1000)
		if($ENGINE_UPTIME - %lbl_bubble_PAN_last_time[$pan_pointer] > $LABEL_WAIT - 5)
			set_control_par($bubble_PAN_id, $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE,$HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
		end if
	end function

	function update_WIDTH_bubble_value
		set_control_par($bubble_WIDTH_id, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, get_control_par(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)/10000)
		set_control_par($bubble_WIDTH_id, $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE,$HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
		set_control_par($bubble_WIDTH_id, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) - 50)
		set_control_par($bubble_WIDTH_id, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y))
		
		%lbl_bubble_PAN_last_time[$pan_pointer] := $ENGINE_UPTIME

		wait($LABEL_WAIT*1000)
		if($ENGINE_UPTIME - %lbl_bubble_PAN_last_time[$pan_pointer] > $LABEL_WAIT - 5)
			set_control_par($bubble_WIDTH_id, $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE,$HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
		end if
	end function

	function tile_Pan
		{description: sets the stereo panorama or width of the channel}
		{variables = $pan_pointer}
		
		$pan_value := get_control_par(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
		

		if ($pan_pointer = $TILE_MASTER)
			{master}
			set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_STEREO,$pan_value/2,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,1)
			set_control_par_str(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_STEREO,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,1))
			if ( $pan_MASTER = 1000000)
				set_control_par_str(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, "Stereo")
			end if
		else
			if ($pan_pointer = $TILE_OHS or $pan_pointer = $TILE_OHM or $pan_pointer = $TILE_ROOM)
				if(%oh_stereo[$pan_pointer] # -1)
					if(%oh_stereo[$pan_pointer] = 1)
						{width}
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_STEREO,$pan_value/2,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$pan_pointer])
						set_control_par_str(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_STEREO, -1, $SPREAD_SLOT, $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$pan_pointer]))
						if ( $pan_OHS = 1000000)
							set_control_par_str(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, "Stereo")
						end if
					else
						{pan}
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_STEREO_PAN,$pan_value,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$pan_pointer])
						set_control_par_str(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_STEREO_PAN,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$pan_pointer]))
					end if
				end if
			else
				set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_STEREO_PAN,$pan_value,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$pan_pointer])
				set_control_par_str(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_STEREO_PAN,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$pan_pointer]))
			end if
		end if
	end function

	on ui_control ($pan_KICK)
		$pan_pointer := $TILE_KICK
		call tile_Pan
		call update_PAN_bubble_value
	end on

	on ui_control ($pan_SNARE)

{MUTE Callbacks}

	function tile_MUTE
		{description: mutes the channel}
		{variables = $mute_pointer}
		$vol_value := get_control_par(%volfader_id[$mute_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
		%mute_state[$mute_pointer] := (get_control_par(%mute_id[$mute_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) + 1) mod 2
		
		if ($mute_pointer = $TILE_REV)
			set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEND_EFFECT_BYPASS,get_control_par(%mute_id[$mute_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE),-1,$REVERB_SLOT,0)
		else
			$vol_value := %solo_state[$mute_pointer]*%mute_state[$mute_pointer]*((%wurzel_zweidrittel[$vol_value]*$cur_volume)/1000)
			set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,$vol_value,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$mute_pointer])
			{set_control_par_str(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME,-1,-1,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$vol_pointer]) & "dB")}
			{set_control_par_str(%mute_id[$mute_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_control_par(%mute_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE))}
			pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND,0,-1)
			pgs_set_key_val(TILE_MUTE_STATE,$mute_pointer,%mute_state[$mute_pointer])
		end if
	end function

	on ui_control ($mute_KICK)
		$mute_pointer := $TILE_KICK
		call tile_MUTE
	end on
	on ui_control ($mute_SNARE)
		$mute_pointer := $TILE_SNARE
		call tile_MUTE

{SOLO Callbacks}
	function tile_SOLO
			{description: solos the channel
				solo_check (0 or 1) if tile other than Reverb is soloed
				rev_check (0 or 1) if Reverb solo is pressed}
			{variables = $solo_pointer}

			%solo_light[$solo_pointer] := get_control_par(%solo_id[$solo_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)

			if($solo_pointer # $TILE_REV)	{update solo_check depending on whether there is a tile soloed or not}
				$c := 0
				$solo_check := 0
				while ($c < $NUM_TILES)
					if ($c # $TILE_REV)
						if (%solo_light[$c] = 1)
							$solo_check := 1
							$c := $NUM_TILES
						end if
					end if
					inc($c)
				end while

				if (get_control_par(%solo_id[$TILE_REV],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) # 1) {if solo REV is not pressed}
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEND_EFFECT_BYPASS, $solo_check, -1, $REVERB_SLOT,0) {bypass the reverb depending on whether there is something soloed or not}
				end if

				$c := 0
				if ($solo_check = 0)
					if ($rev_check = 1)
						$c := 0
						while($c < $NUM_TILES)
							if (%Tile_has_Mixer[$c] = $YES)
								if ($c # $TILE_REV and $c # $TILE_MASTER)
									set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME,((%solo_state[3] + 1) mod 2)*631000,-1,-1,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$c])
								end if
							end if
							inc($c)
						end while
					else
						$c := 0
						while ($c < $NUM_TILES)
							%solo_state[$c] := 1
							inc($c)
						end while
					end if
				else
					while ($c < $NUM_TILES)
						%solo_state[$c] := %solo_light[$c]
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME, 631000,-1,-1,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$c])
						inc($c)
					end while
				end if

				$c := 0
				while($c < $NUM_TILES)
					if (%Tile_has_Mixer[$c] = $YES)
						$vol_value := get_control_par(%volfader_id[$c], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,%solo_state[$c]*%mute_state[$c]*((%wurzel_zweidrittel[$vol_value]*$cur_volume)/1000),-1,$SPREAD_SLOT, $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$c])
					end if
					inc($c)
				end while
			else 	{Reverb}
				%solo_light[$solo_pointer] := get_control_par(%solo_id[$solo_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
				%solo_state[$solo_pointer] := %solo_light[$solo_pointer]
				
				$rev_check := get_control_par(%solo_id[$solo_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
				
				if ($solo_check = 0)
					if ($rev_check = 1)
						$c := 0
						while($c < $NUM_TILES)
							if (%Tile_has_Mixer[$c] = $YES)
								if ($c # $TILE_REV and $c # $TILE_MASTER)
									set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME,((%solo_state[3] + 1) mod 2)*631000,-1,-1,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$c])
								end if
							end if
							inc($c)
						end while
					else 	{uncheck rev solo while no other solo present}
						$c := 0
						while ($c < $NUM_TILES)
							%solo_state[$c] := 1
							inc($c)
						end while
						$c := 0
						while($c < $NUM_TILES)
							if (%Tile_has_Mixer[$c] = $YES)
								if ($c # $TILE_REV and $c # $TILE_MASTER)
									set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME, 631000,-1,-1,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$c])
								end if
								$vol_value := get_control_par(%volfader_id[$c], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,%solo_state[$c]*%mute_state[$c]*((%wurzel_zweidrittel[$vol_value]*$cur_volume)/1000),-1,$SPREAD_SLOT, $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$c])
							end if
							inc($c)
						end while						
					end if
				else
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEND_EFFECT_BYPASS, $solo_check * ((%solo_state[3] + 1) mod 2), -1, $REVERB_SLOT,0)
					if ($rev_check = 1)
						$c := 0
						while($c < $NUM_TILES)
							if (%Tile_has_Mixer[$c] = $YES)
								if ($c # $TILE_REV and $c # $TILE_MASTER)
									set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME, 631000,-1,-1,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$c])
								end if
								$vol_value := get_control_par(%volfader_id[$c], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,%solo_state[$c]*%mute_state[$c]*((%wurzel_zweidrittel[$vol_value]*$cur_volume)/1000),-1,$SPREAD_SLOT, $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$c])
							end if
							inc($c)
						end while
					else
						$c := 0
						while($c < $NUM_TILES)
							if (%Tile_has_Mixer[$c] = $YES)
								if ($c # $TILE_REV and $c # $TILE_MASTER)
									$vol_value := get_control_par(%volfader_id[$c], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
									set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,%solo_state[$c]*%mute_state[$c]*((%wurzel_zweidrittel[$vol_value]*$cur_volume)/1000),-1,$SPREAD_SLOT, $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$c])
								end if

							end if
							inc($c)
						end while
					end if
				end if	

			end if
		end function

	on ui_control ($solo_KICK)
		$solo_pointer := $TILE_KICK
		call tile_SOLO
	end on
	on ui_control ($solo_SNARE)

{GROOVE Callbacks}
	on ui_control ($play_btn)
		$playing_flag := 0
		$key_counter := $play_btn
		pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, -1)
		pgs_set_key_val(GROOVE_ACTION, 0, $play_btn)
		pgs_set_key_val(GROOVE_ACTION, 1, 0)
		pgs_set_key_val(GROOVE_ACTION, 2, 0)
		pgs_set_key_val(GROOVE_ACTION, 3, 0)
		pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, 2)
	end on

	on ui_control ($prev_groove)
		pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, -1)
		pgs_set_key_val(GROOVE_ACTION, 0, -1)
		pgs_set_key_val(GROOVE_ACTION, 1, 1)
		pgs_set_key_val(GROOVE_ACTION, 2, 0)
		pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, 2)
		$prev_groove := 0
	end on

	on ui_control ($next_groove)
		pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, -1)
		pgs_set_key_val(GROOVE_ACTION, 0, -1)
		pgs_set_key_val(GROOVE_ACTION, 1, 0)
		pgs_set_key_val(GROOVE_ACTION, 2, 1)
		pgs_set_key_val(GROOVE_ACTION, 3, 0)
		pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, 2)
		$next_groove := 0
	end on
	{/Groove Callbacks}

{SOUND PRESETS - CALLBACKS / FUNCTIONS}

	function update_sound_preset_menu
		{hide all}
		$arr_count_1 := 0
		while ($arr_count_1 < 7)
			set_control_par(%sound_preset_controls[$arr_count_1],      $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
			set_control_par(%sound_preset_controls[$arr_count_1 + 11], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
			inc($arr_count_1)
		end while

		{show selected}
		set_control_par(%sound_preset_controls[$Preset_Category],      $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
		set_control_par(%sound_preset_controls[$Preset_Category + 11], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)

		if($category_mnu < $NUM_CATEGORIES - 1)
			set_control_par_str(%sound_preset_controls[10],$CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE,"header-preset-delete-btn-disabled")
		else
			set_control_par_str(%sound_preset_controls[10],$CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE,"header-preset-delete-btn")
		end if

		select ($Preset_Category)
			case $FACTORY_PRESET_CAT_1
				@fact_sound_preset_name_1 := get_menu_item_str(%sound_preset_controls[00],$fact_sound_preset_menu_1)
				$active_preset := $fact_sound_preset_menu_1
			case $FACTORY_PRESET_CAT_2
				@fact_sound_preset_name_2 := get_menu_item_str(%sound_preset_controls[01],$fact_sound_preset_menu_2 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_1	)
				$active_preset := $fact_sound_preset_menu_2
			case $FACTORY_PRESET_CAT_3
				@fact_sound_preset_name_3 := get_menu_item_str(%sound_preset_controls[02],$fact_sound_preset_menu_3 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_1	- $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_2)
				$active_preset := $fact_sound_preset_menu_3
			case $FACTORY_PRESET_CAT_4
				@fact_sound_preset_name_4 := get_menu_item_str(%sound_preset_controls[03],$fact_sound_preset_menu_4 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_1	- $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_2 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_3	)
				$active_preset := $fact_sound_preset_menu_4
			case $FACTORY_PRESET_CAT_5
				@fact_sound_preset_name_5 := get_menu_item_str(%sound_preset_controls[04],$fact_sound_preset_menu_5 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_1 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_2 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_3 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_4)
				$active_preset := $fact_sound_preset_menu_5
			case $FACTORY_PRESET_CAT_6
				@fact_sound_preset_name_6 := get_menu_item_str(%sound_preset_controls[05],$fact_sound_preset_menu_6 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_1 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_2 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_3 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_4 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_5)
				$active_preset := $fact_sound_preset_menu_6
			case $USER_PRESET_CAT
				$active_preset := $user_sound_preset_menu
				if (%user_num_snd_Presets[0] > 0)
					@user_sound_preset_name := !user_sound_preset_names[$active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS]
				else
					@user_sound_preset_name := "No Saved Preset"
				end if
		end select
	end function

	function reset_instrument
		
		$reset_flag := 1
		fade_out($ALL_EVENTS,5000,0)
		wait(5000)

		$tile_count := 0
		while ($tile_count < $NUM_TILES)
			if (%Tile_has_Mixer[$tile_count] = $YES)
				if ($tile_count = $TILE_MASTER)
					$bus_index := 1
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_TR_ATTACK,%master_fx_data[$MAST_TRANS_ATTACK], -1, $TRANS1_SLOT, $bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_TR_SUSTAIN,%master_fx_data[$MAST_TRANS_RELEASE], -1, $TRANS1_SLOT, $bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SCOMP_THRESHOLD,%master_fx_data[$MAST_COMP_THRES],-1,$COMP_SLOT,$bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SCOMP_ATTACK,%master_fx_data[$MAST_COMP_ATTACK],-1,$COMP_SLOT,$bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SCOMP_RATIO,%master_fx_data[$MAST_COMP_RATIO],-1,$COMP_SLOT,$bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SCOMP_MAKEUP,%master_fx_data[$MAST_COMP_MAKEUP],-1,$COMP_SLOT,$bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SHAPE,%master_fx_data[$MAST_SAT_GAIN],-1,$SAT_SLOT,$bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,%master_fx_data[$MAST_SAT_LEVEL],-1,$SAT_SLOT,$bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_LF_FREQ,%master_fx_data[$MAST_EQ_LOW_FREQ],-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_LF_GAIN,%master_fx_data[$MAST_EQ_LOW_GAIN],-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_HMF_FREQ,%master_fx_data[$MAST_EQ_MID_FREQ],-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_HMF_GAIN,%master_fx_data[$MAST_EQ_MID_GAIN],-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_HF_FREQ,%master_fx_data[$MAST_EQ_HI_FREQ],-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_HF_GAIN,%master_fx_data[$MAST_EQ_HI_GAIN],-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_EFFECT_BYPASS,(%master_onoff_data[0] + 1) mod 2, -1, $TRANS1_SLOT, $bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_EFFECT_BYPASS,(%master_onoff_data[1] + 1) mod 2, -1, $COMP_SLOT, $bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_EFFECT_BYPASS,(%master_onoff_data[2] + 1) mod 2, -1, $SAT_SLOT, $bus_index)
					set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_EFFECT_BYPASS,(%master_onoff_data[3] + 1) mod 2, -1, $EQ1_SLOT, $bus_index)
					call update_MASTER_FX_Values
					$vol_pointer := $tile_count
					call tile_Volume
					$pan_pointer  := $tile_count
					call tile_Pan
				else
					if ($tile_count = $TILE_REV)
						call reverbpicupdate
						call irload
						$solo_pointer := $tile_count
						call tile_SOLO
						$mute_pointer := $tile_count
						call tile_MUTE
						$vol_pointer := $tile_count
						call tile_Volume
					else
						$bus_index := $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$tile_count]
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_TR_ATTACK,%fx_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $TRANS_ATTACK],-1,$TRANS1_SLOT,$bus_index)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_TR_SUSTAIN,%fx_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $TRANS_RELEASE],-1,$TRANS1_SLOT,$bus_index)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_FCOMP_INPUT,  %ingain[%fx_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $COMP_AMOUNT]],-1, $COMP_SLOT,$bus_index)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_FCOMP_MAKEUP, %outgain[%fx_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $COMP_AMOUNT]], -1 ,$COMP_SLOT,$bus_index)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_FCOMP_ATTACK, %fx_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $COMP_ATTACK],  -1, $COMP_SLOT,$bus_index)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SHAPE,%fx_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $SAT_GAIN],-1,$SAT_SLOT,$bus_index)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,%fx_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $SAT_LEVEL],-1,$SAT_SLOT,$bus_index)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_LF_FREQ,%fx_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $EQ_LOW_FREQ],-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_LF_GAIN,%fx_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $EQ_LOW_GAIN],-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_HMF_FREQ,%fx_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $EQ_MID_FREQ],-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_HMF_GAIN,%fx_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $EQ_MID_GAIN],-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_HF_FREQ,%fx_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $EQ_HI_FREQ],-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_HF_GAIN,%fx_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $EQ_HI_GAIN],-1,$EQ1_SLOT,$bus_index)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_EFFECT_BYPASS,(%onoff_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_ONOFF) + 0] + 1) mod 2, -1, $TRANS1_SLOT, $bus_index)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_EFFECT_BYPASS,(%onoff_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_ONOFF) + 1] + 1) mod 2, -1, $COMP_SLOT, $bus_index)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_EFFECT_BYPASS,(%onoff_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_ONOFF) + 2] + 1) mod 2, -1, $SAT_SLOT, $bus_index)
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_EFFECT_BYPASS,(%onoff_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_ONOFF) + 3] + 1) mod 2, -1, $EQ1_SLOT, $bus_index)
						call update_FX_Values
						$vol_pointer  := $tile_count
						call tile_Volume
						$pan_pointer  := $tile_count
						call tile_Pan
						$solo_pointer := $tile_count
						call tile_SOLO
						$mute_pointer := $tile_count
						call tile_MUTE

						{reverb_send}
						$send_value := %fx_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $RVB_SEND]
						if($send_value < 500)
							$send_value := $send_value * 1260
						else
							if($send_value = 500)
								$send_value := 630000
							else
								$send_value := 630000 + (328*($send_value - 500))
							end if
						end if
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_SENDLEVEL_0,$send_value,-1,$SEND_SLOT,$bus_index)

					end if
				end if
			end if

			if (%Tile_has_Ac_Layers[$tile_count] = $YES)
				
				$inst_count := %Tile_to_Inst_remap[$tile_count]
				
				{Ac_El BALANCE}
					if (%Tile_has_El_Layers[$tile_count] = $YES)
						$math_Input := $BAL_MIDWAY_VOL * %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_EL_BAL]
						call equal_power
						$ac_vol := ($math_Output + 50) / 100 + %equal_gain[%src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_EL_BAL]]

						$math_Input := $BAL_MIDWAY_VOL * (10000 - %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_EL_BAL])
						call equal_power
						$el_vol := ($math_Output + 50) / 100 + %equal_gain[%src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_EL_BAL]]

						if (%Tile_DOES_NOT_have_EL_Layers[$tile_count] = $YES)
							$ac_vol := 500000
						end if

						
						$x := %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count] * 8
						while ($x < %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count + 1] * 8)
							if (%AC_GROUP_DATA[$x] > -1)
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME, $ac_vol, %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x], -1, -1)
								$y := 1
								while ($y < %Ac_Layer_per_Tile[$tile_count])
									set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME, $ac_vol, %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x] + $y , -1, -1)
									inc($y)
								end while
							end if
							inc($x)
						end while

						$a := %EL_GROUP_DATA[$inst_count]
						while ($a < %EL_GROUP_DATA[$inst_count + 1])
							set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_VOLUME, $el_vol, $a, -1, -1)
							inc($a)
						end while

					end if
				{/Ac_El BALANCE}

				{Ac_Tune}
					$x := %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count] * 8
					while ($x < %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count + 1] * 8)
						if (%AC_GROUP_DATA[$x] > -1)
							set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_TUNE, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_TUNE], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x], -1, -1)
							$y := 1
							while ($y < %Ac_Layer_per_Tile[$tile_count])
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_TUNE, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_TUNE], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x] + $y , -1, -1)
								inc($y)
							end while
						end if
						inc($x)
					end while
				{/Ac_Tune}

				{Out/Sub}
					if ($tile_count = $TILE_KICK or $tile_count = $TILE_SNARE)
						$math_Input := $MIC_MIDWAY_VOL * (10000 - %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_MIC_BAL])
						call equal_power
						$temp_vol_1 := ($math_Output + 50) / 100 + %equal_gain[%src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_MIC_BAL]]

						$math_Input := $MIC_MIDWAY_VOL * %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_MIC_BAL]
						call equal_power
						$temp_vol_2 := ($math_Output + 50) / 100 + %equal_gain[%src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_MIC_BAL]]
					end if

					$x := %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count]
					while ($x < %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count + 1])
						if (%AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 1] > -1)
							set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, $temp_vol_1, %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 0], $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
							set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, $temp_vol_2, %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 1], $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
							$y := 1
							while ($y < %Ac_Layer_per_Tile[$tile_count])
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, $temp_vol_1, %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 0] + $y, $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, $temp_vol_2, %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 1] + $y, $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
								inc($y)
							end while
						end if
						inc($x)
					end while
					
					{voice optimization}
					select ($tile_count)
						case $TILE_KICK	
							if ($temp_vol_1 > $temp_vol_2)
								$mic_pointer := 1
								if ($temp_vol_2 < 100000)
									pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND,0,-1)
									pgs_set_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer, 0)
									%mic_balance_state[$mic_pointer] := pgs_get_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer)
								else
									pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND,0,-1)
									pgs_set_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer, 1)
									%mic_balance_state[$mic_pointer] := pgs_get_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer)
								end if
							else
								$mic_pointer := 0
								if ($temp_vol_1 < 100000)
									pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND,0,-1)
									pgs_set_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer, 0)
									%mic_balance_state[$mic_pointer] := pgs_get_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer)
								else
									pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND,0,-1)
									pgs_set_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer, 1)
									%mic_balance_state[$mic_pointer] := pgs_get_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer)
								end if
							end if
						case $TILE_SNARE	
							if ($temp_vol_1 > $temp_vol_2)
								$mic_pointer := 4
								if ($temp_vol_2 < 100000)
									pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND,0,-1)
									pgs_set_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer, 0)
									%mic_balance_state[$mic_pointer] := pgs_get_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer)
								else
									pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND,0,-1)
									pgs_set_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer, 1)
									%mic_balance_state[$mic_pointer] := pgs_get_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer)
								end if
							else
								$mic_pointer := 3
								if ($temp_vol_1 < 100000)
									pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND,0,-1)
									pgs_set_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer, 0)
									%mic_balance_state[$mic_pointer] := pgs_get_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer)
								else
									pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND,0,-1)
									pgs_set_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer, 1)
									%mic_balance_state[$mic_pointer] := pgs_get_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer)
								end if
							end if
					end select
				{/Out/Sub}

				{OH-ROOM}
					if ($tile_count = $TILE_PERC1 or $tile_count = $TILE_PERC2 or $tile_count = $TILE_PERC3 or $tile_count = $TILE_PERC4 or $tile_count = $TILE_PERC5)
						$x := %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count]
						while ($x < %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count + 1])
							if (%AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 4] > -1)
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_ROOM_LEVEL], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 4], $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_ROOM_LEVEL], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 5], $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_PERC_PLATE],    %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 6], $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
								$y := 1
								while ($y < %Ac_Layer_per_Tile[$tile_count])
									set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_ROOM_LEVEL], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 4] + $y , $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
									set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_ROOM_LEVEL], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 5] + $y , $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
									set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_PERC_PLATE],    %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 6] + $y , $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
									inc($y)
								end while
							end if
							inc($x)
						end while
					else
						$x := %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count]
						while ($x < %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count + 1])
							if (%AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 4] > -1)
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_ROOM_LEVEL], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 4], $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_ROOM_LEVEL], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 5], $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_ROOM_LEVEL], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 6], $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
								$y := 1
								while ($y < %Ac_Layer_per_Tile[$tile_count])
									set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_ROOM_LEVEL], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 4] + $y , $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
									set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_ROOM_LEVEL], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 5] + $y , $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
									set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_ROOM_LEVEL], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 6] + $y , $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
									inc($y)
								end while
							end if
							inc($x)
						end while
						{voice optimizing}
						if (%src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_ROOM_LEVEL] < 16542)
							pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, -1)
							pgs_set_key_val(KIT_VOICE_ALLOW, $inst_count, 0)
							%save_kit_voice_allow[$inst_count] := 0
						else
							pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, -1)
							pgs_set_key_val(KIT_VOICE_ALLOW, $inst_count, 1)
							%save_kit_voice_allow[$inst_count] := 1
						end if
					end if
				{/OH-ROOM}

				{TRASH LEVEL}
					$x := %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count]
					while ($x < %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count + 1])
						if (%AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 2] > -1)
							set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_TRASH], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 2], $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
							$y := 1
							while ($y < %Ac_Layer_per_Tile[$tile_count])
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_TRASH], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x * 8 + 2] + $y, $GAIN_SLOT, -1)
								inc($y)
							end while
						end if
						inc($x)
					end while

					select ($tile_count)
						case $TILE_KICK
							$mic_pointer := 2
							if ($ac_trash_level < 20000)
								pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND,0,-1)
								pgs_set_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer, 0)
								%mic_balance_state[$mic_pointer] := pgs_get_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer)
							else
								pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND,0,-1)
								pgs_set_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer, 1)
								%mic_balance_state[$mic_pointer] := pgs_get_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer)
							end if
						case $TILE_SNARE
							$mic_pointer := 5
							if ($ac_trash_level < 20000)
								pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND,0,-1)
								pgs_set_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer, 0)
								%mic_balance_state[$mic_pointer] := pgs_get_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer)
							else
								pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND,0,-1)
								pgs_set_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer, 1)
								%mic_balance_state[$mic_pointer] := pgs_get_key_val(MIC_VOICE_ALLOW, $mic_pointer)
							end if
					end select
				{/TRASH LEVEL}

				{Ac_Attack}
					$x := %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count] * 8
					while ($x < %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count + 1] * 8)
						if (%AC_GROUP_DATA[$x] > -1)
							set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_ATTACK, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_ATTACK], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x], find_mod(%AC_GROUP_DATA[$x], "ENV_AHDSR"), -1)
							$y := 1
							while ($y < %Ac_Layer_per_Tile[$tile_count])
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_ATTACK, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_ATTACK], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x] + $y , find_mod(%AC_GROUP_DATA[$x] + $y , "ENV_AHDSR"), -1)
								inc($y)
							end while
						end if
						inc($x)
					end while
				{/Ac_Attack}

				{Ac_Hold}
					$x := %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count] * 8
					while ($x < %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count + 1] * 8)
						if (%AC_GROUP_DATA[$x] > -1)
							set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_HOLD, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_HOLD], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x], find_mod(%AC_GROUP_DATA[$x], "ENV_AHDSR"), -1)
							$y := 1
							while ($y < %Ac_Layer_per_Tile[$tile_count])
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_HOLD, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_HOLD], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x] + $y , find_mod(%AC_GROUP_DATA[$x] + $y , "ENV_AHDSR"), -1)
								inc($y)
							end while
						end if
						inc($x)
					end while
				{/Ac-Hold}

				{Ac_Decay}
					$x := %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count] * 8
					while ($x < %AC_INSTRUMENT_OFFSET[$inst_count + 1] * 8)
						if (%AC_GROUP_DATA[$x] > -1)
							set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_DECAY, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_DECAY], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x], find_mod(%AC_GROUP_DATA[$x], "ENV_AHDSR"), -1)
							$y := 1
							while ($y < %Ac_Layer_per_Tile[$tile_count])
								set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_DECAY, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_AC_DECAY], %AC_GROUP_DATA[$x] + $y , find_mod(%AC_GROUP_DATA[$x] + $y , "ENV_AHDSR"), -1)
								inc($y)
							end while
						end if
						inc($x)
					end while
				{/Ac_Decay}

				{Ac_Inst_SWITCH}
					set_control_par(%Ac_src_Pic_id[$tile_count],    $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE,	%Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
					set_control_par(%Ac_Layer_Menu_id[$tile_count], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE,			%Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
					pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, -1)
					select ($tile_count)
						case $TILE_KICK
							pgs_set_key_val(ACTIVE_KICK,  0, %Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_SNARE
							pgs_set_key_val(ACTIVE_SNARE, 0, %Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_HIHAT
							pgs_set_key_val(ACTIVE_HIHAT, 0, %Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_TOM1
							pgs_set_key_val(ACTIVE_TOM1,  0, %Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_TOM2
							pgs_set_key_val(ACTIVE_TOM2,  0, %Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_TOM3
							pgs_set_key_val(ACTIVE_TOM3,  0, %Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_CYMB1
							pgs_set_key_val(ACTIVE_CYMB1, 0, %Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_CYMB2
							pgs_set_key_val(ACTIVE_CYMB2, 0, %Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_CYMB3
							pgs_set_key_val(ACTIVE_CYMB3, 0, %Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_PERC1
							pgs_set_key_val(ACTIVE_PERC1, 0, %Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_PERC2
							pgs_set_key_val(ACTIVE_PERC2, 0, %Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_PERC3
							pgs_set_key_val(ACTIVE_PERC3, 0, %Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_PERC4
							pgs_set_key_val(ACTIVE_PERC4, 0, %Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_PERC5
							pgs_set_key_val(ACTIVE_PERC5, 0, %Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
					end select
				{/Ac_Inst_SWITCH}

				{AC_PURGE_SYSTEM_update}
					pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, -1)
					$group_count := 0
					while ($group_count < $AC_NUM_GROUPS)
						pgs_set_key_val(AC_LOAD_PURGE_STATE, $group_count, %Ac_Group_PURGE_State[$group_count])
						inc($group_count)
						wait(1)   
					end while
					pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, 0)
				{/AC_Global_PURGE_SYSTEM}
			end if

			if (%Tile_has_El_Layers[$tile_count] = $YES)
				
				{El_Tune}
					$a := %EL_GROUP_DATA[$inst_count]
					while ($a < %EL_GROUP_DATA[$inst_count + 1])
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_TUNE, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_EL_TUNE], $a, -1, -1)
						inc($a)
					end while
				{/El_Tune}

				{El_DUAL_Filter}
				    if (%src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_EL_FILTER] <= 0)
				        $cutof_freq := 1000000 - abs(%src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_EL_FILTER])

				        $a := %EL_GROUP_DATA[$inst_count]
				        while ($a < %EL_GROUP_DATA[$inst_count + 1])
					        set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_CUTOFF,$cutof_freq,     													$a, $FX_SLOT_LP, -1)
					        set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_CUTOFF,%src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_EL_FILTER], $a, $FX_SLOT_HP, -1)
				        	inc($a)
				        end while
				    else
				    	$a := %EL_GROUP_DATA[$inst_count]
				        while ($a < %EL_GROUP_DATA[$inst_count + 1])
					        set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_CUTOFF,$el_dual_Filter, $a, $FX_SLOT_HP, -1)
				        	inc($a)
				        end while
				    end if
				{/El_DUAL_Filter}

				{El_Trig_Delay}
					pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, -1)
					pgs_set_key_val(ELEC_DELAY, %Tile_to_Inst_remap[$tile_count], %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_EL_DELAY])

					{special case for open HH}
					$opn_HH_pgs_value := %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_EL_DELAY]
					pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, -1)
					pgs_set_key_val(ELEC_DELAY_OPN_HH, 0, $opn_HH_pgs_value)
				{/El_Trig_Delay}

				{El_Attack}
					$a := %EL_GROUP_DATA[$inst_count]
			        while ($a < %EL_GROUP_DATA[$inst_count + 1])
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_ATTACK, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_EL_ATTACK], $a, find_mod($a, "ENV_AHDSR"), -1)
			        	inc($a)
			        end while
				{/El_Attack}

				{El_Hold}
					$a := %EL_GROUP_DATA[$inst_count]
			        while ($a < %EL_GROUP_DATA[$inst_count + 1])
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_HOLD, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_EL_HOLD], $a, find_mod($a, "ENV_AHDSR"), -1)
			        	inc($a)
			        end while
				{/El_Hold}

				{El_Decay}
					$a := %EL_GROUP_DATA[$inst_count]
			        while ($a < %EL_GROUP_DATA[$inst_count + 1])
						set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_DECAY, %src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $SRC_EL_DECAY], $a, find_mod($a, "ENV_AHDSR"), -1)
			        	inc($a)
			        end while
				{/El_Decay}

				{El_Inst_SWITCH}
					set_control_par(%El_src_Pic_id[$tile_count],    $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, %El_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
					set_control_par(%El_Layer_Menu_id[$tile_count], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE,			%El_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
					pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, -1)
					select ($tile_count)
						case $TILE_KICK
							pgs_set_key_val(ELEC_ACTIVE_KICK,  0, %El_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_SNARE
							pgs_set_key_val(ELEC_ACTIVE_SNARE, 0, %El_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_HIHAT
							pgs_set_key_val(ELEC_ACTIVE_HIHAT, 0, %El_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_TOM1
							pgs_set_key_val(ELEC_ACTIVE_TOM1,  0, %El_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_TOM2
							pgs_set_key_val(ELEC_ACTIVE_TOM2,  0, %El_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
						case $TILE_TOM3
							pgs_set_key_val(ELEC_ACTIVE_TOM3,  0, %El_Inst_Selection[$tile_count])
					end select
				{/El_Inst_SWITCH}

				{EL_Global_PURGE_SYSTEM}
					pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, -1)
					$group_count := 0
					while ($group_count < $EL_NUM_GROUPS)
						pgs_set_key_val(EL_LOAD_PURGE_STATE, $group_count, %El_Group_PURGE_State[$group_count])
						inc($group_count)
						wait(1)   
					end while
					pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, 0)
				{/AC_Global_PURGE_SYSTEM}
			end if
			
			$tile_pointer := $tile_count
			call update_SOURCE_Values

			inc($tile_count)
		end while
		$reset_flag := 0
		fade_in($ALL_EVENTS,5000)
	end function

	function load_sound_preset
		fade_out($ALL_EVENTS,5000,0)
		wait(5000)   
		$sound_preset_flag := 0

		select ($Preset_Category)

			case $FACTORY_PRESET_CAT_1
				$last_sound_preset			:= $fact_sound_preset_menu_1
				$active_preset				:= $fact_sound_preset_menu_1
				@fact_sound_preset_name_1	:= get_menu_item_str(%sound_preset_controls[00],$fact_sound_preset_menu_1)
			case $FACTORY_PRESET_CAT_2
				$last_sound_preset			:= $fact_sound_preset_menu_2
				$active_preset				:= $fact_sound_preset_menu_2
				@fact_sound_preset_name_2	:= get_menu_item_str(%sound_preset_controls[01],$fact_sound_preset_menu_2 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_1)
			case $FACTORY_PRESET_CAT_3
				$last_sound_preset			:= $fact_sound_preset_menu_3
				$active_preset				:= $fact_sound_preset_menu_3
				@fact_sound_preset_name_3	:= get_menu_item_str(%sound_preset_controls[02],$fact_sound_preset_menu_3 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_1 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_2)
			case $FACTORY_PRESET_CAT_4
				$last_sound_preset			:= $fact_sound_preset_menu_4
				$active_preset				:= $fact_sound_preset_menu_4
				@fact_sound_preset_name_4	:= get_menu_item_str(%sound_preset_controls[03],$fact_sound_preset_menu_4 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_1 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_2 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_3)
			case $FACTORY_PRESET_CAT_5
				$last_sound_preset			:= $fact_sound_preset_menu_5
				$active_preset				:= $fact_sound_preset_menu_5
				@fact_sound_preset_name_5	:= get_menu_item_str(%sound_preset_controls[04],$fact_sound_preset_menu_5 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_1 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_2 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_3 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_4)
			case $FACTORY_PRESET_CAT_6
				$last_sound_preset			:= $fact_sound_preset_menu_6
				$active_preset				:= $fact_sound_preset_menu_6
				@fact_sound_preset_name_6	:= get_menu_item_str(%sound_preset_controls[05],$fact_sound_preset_menu_6 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_1 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_2 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_3 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_4 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_5)
			case $USER_PRESET_CAT
				$last_sound_preset			:= $user_sound_preset_menu
				$active_preset				:= $user_sound_preset_menu
				if (%user_num_snd_Presets[0] > 0)
					@user_sound_preset_name := !user_sound_preset_names[$active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS]
				else
					@user_sound_preset_name := "No Saved Preset"
				end if
		end select

		{Master has no mute/solo but has L<->R swap button AND MASTER FX CHAIN}
		{REVERB has Volume, Solo MUTE and ir_value & ir_category but NO FX}
		
		{message("last preset: " & $last_sound_preset & " - active: " & $active_preset & " - Preset Bank: " & $Preset_Category)}

		if ($active_preset < $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS)
			{FACTORY Settings}
			$tile_count := 0
			while($tile_count < $NUM_TILES)

				if (%Tile_has_Mixer[$tile_count] = $YES)
					set_control_par(%volfader_id[$tile_count],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE,%fact_snd_preset_vol[($active_preset * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count])

					if($tile_count = $TILE_MASTER)
						$lr_swap := %fact_snd_preset_mute[($active_preset * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count]
						set_control_par(%pan_id[$tile_count],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE,%fact_snd_preset_pan[($active_preset * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count])
					else
						if ($tile_count # $TILE_REV)
							set_control_par(%mute_id[$tile_count], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %fact_snd_preset_mute[($active_preset * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count])
							set_control_par(%solo_id[$tile_count], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %fact_snd_preset_solo[($active_preset * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count])
							set_control_par( %pan_id[$tile_count], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE,  %fact_snd_preset_pan[($active_preset * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count]) 
						else
							set_control_par(%mute_id[$tile_count], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %fact_snd_preset_mute[($active_preset * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count])
							set_control_par(%solo_id[$tile_count], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %fact_snd_preset_solo[($active_preset * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count])
							$ir_category := %fact_snd_preset_reverb[($active_preset * $NUM_CONTROLS_REVERB)]
							set_control_par(%reverb_controls[$ir_category],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE,%fact_snd_preset_reverb[($active_preset * $NUM_CONTROLS_REVERB) + 1])
						end if
					end if

					$tile_count_2 := 0
					while($tile_count_2 < $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) 
						%fx_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $tile_count_2] := %fact_snd_preset_fx_data[($active_preset * $NUM_TILES * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + ($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $tile_count_2]
						inc($tile_count_2)
					end while

					$tile_count_2 := 0
					while($tile_count_2 < $NUM_CONTROLS_ONOFF) 
						%onoff_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_ONOFF) + $tile_count_2] := %fact_snd_preset_fx_onoff[($active_preset * $NUM_TILES * $NUM_CONTROLS_ONOFF) + ($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_ONOFF) + $tile_count_2]
						inc($tile_count_2)
					end while
				end if

				if (%Tile_has_Ac_Layers[$tile_count] = $YES)
					$tile_count_2 := 0
					while($tile_count_2 < $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) 
						%src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $tile_count_2] := %fact_snd_preset_src_data[($active_preset * $NUM_TILES * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + ($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $tile_count_2]
						inc($tile_count_2)
					end while
				end if

				$tile_count_2 := 0
				while($tile_count_2 < $NUM_CONTROLS_MASTER_FX)
					%master_fx_data[$tile_count_2] := %fact_snd_preset_master_fx[($active_preset * $NUM_CONTROLS_MASTER_FX) + $tile_count_2]
					inc($tile_count_2)
				end while
				
				$tile_count_2 := 0
				while($tile_count_2 < $NUM_CONTROLS_MASTER_FX_ONOFF)
					%master_onoff_data[$tile_count_2] := %fact_snd_preset_master_fx_onoff[($active_preset * $NUM_CONTROLS_MASTER_FX_ONOFF) + $tile_count_2]
					inc($tile_count_2)
				end while

				$tile_count_2 := 0
				while($tile_count_2 < $NUM_TILES)
					%Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count_2] := %fact_snd_preset_Ac_Selection[($active_preset * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count_2]
					inc($tile_count_2)
				end while

				$tile_count_2 := 0
				while($tile_count_2 < $NUM_TILES)
					%El_Inst_Selection[$tile_count_2] := %fact_snd_preset_El_Selection[($active_preset * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count_2]
					inc($tile_count_2)
				end while

				$tile_count_2 := 0
				while($tile_count_2 < $AC_NUM_GROUPS)
					%Ac_Group_PURGE_State[$tile_count_2] := %fact_snd_preset_Ac_Group_PURGE[($active_preset * $AC_NUM_GROUPS) + $tile_count_2]
					inc($tile_count_2)
				end while

				$tile_count_2 := 0
				while($tile_count_2 < $EL_NUM_GROUPS)
					%El_Group_PURGE_State[$tile_count_2] := %fact_snd_preset_El_Group_PURGE[($active_preset * $EL_NUM_GROUPS) + $tile_count_2]
					inc($tile_count_2)
				end while

				inc($tile_count)
			end while
		else
			{USER Settings}
			$tile_count := 0
			while($tile_count < $NUM_TILES)
				
				if (%Tile_has_Mixer[$tile_count] > 0)
					set_control_par(%volfader_id[$tile_count],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %user_snd_preset_vol[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count])
					if($tile_count = $TILE_MASTER)
						$lr_swap := %user_snd_preset_mute[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count]
						set_control_par(%pan_id[$tile_count],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE,%user_snd_preset_pan[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count])
					else
						if ($tile_count # $TILE_REV)
							set_control_par(%mute_id[$tile_count], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %user_snd_preset_mute[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count])
							set_control_par(%solo_id[$tile_count], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %user_snd_preset_solo[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count])
							set_control_par( %pan_id[$tile_count], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE,  %user_snd_preset_pan[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count]) 
						else
							set_control_par(%mute_id[$tile_count], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %user_snd_preset_mute[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count])
							set_control_par(%solo_id[$tile_count], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %user_snd_preset_solo[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count])
							$ir_category := %user_snd_preset_reverb[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_CONTROLS_REVERB)]
							set_control_par(%reverb_controls[$ir_category],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE,%user_snd_preset_reverb[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_CONTROLS_REVERB) + 1])
						end if
					end if
				end if

				$tile_count_2 := 0
				while($tile_count_2 < $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) 
					%src_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $tile_count_2] := %user_snd_preset_src_data[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_TILES * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + ($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_SOURCE) + $tile_count_2]
					inc($tile_count_2)
				end while

				$tile_count_2 := 0
				while($tile_count_2 < $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) 
					%fx_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $tile_count_2] := %user_snd_preset_fx_data[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_TILES * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + ($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_FX) + $tile_count_2]
					inc($tile_count_2)
				end while

				$tile_count_2 := 0
				while($tile_count_2 < $NUM_CONTROLS_ONOFF) 
					%onoff_data[($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_ONOFF) + $tile_count_2] := %user_snd_preset_fx_onoff[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_TILES * $NUM_CONTROLS_ONOFF) + ($tile_count * $NUM_CONTROLS_ONOFF) + $tile_count_2]
					inc($tile_count_2)
				end while

				$tile_count_2 := 0
				while($tile_count_2 < $NUM_CONTROLS_MASTER_FX)
					%master_fx_data[$tile_count_2] := %user_snd_preset_master_fx[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_CONTROLS_MASTER_FX) + $tile_count_2]
					inc($tile_count_2)
				end while
				
				$tile_count_2 := 0
				while($tile_count_2 < $NUM_CONTROLS_MASTER_FX_ONOFF)
					%master_onoff_data[$tile_count_2] := %user_snd_preset_master_fx_onoff[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_CONTROLS_MASTER_FX_ONOFF) + $tile_count_2]
					inc($tile_count_2)
				end while

				$tile_count_2 := 0
				while($tile_count_2 < $NUM_TILES)
					%Ac_Inst_Selection[$tile_count_2] := %user_snd_preset_Ac_Selection[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count_2]
					inc($tile_count_2)
				end while

				$tile_count_2 := 0
				while($tile_count_2 < $NUM_TILES)
					%El_Inst_Selection[$tile_count_2] := %user_snd_preset_El_Selection[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_TILES) + $tile_count_2]
					inc($tile_count_2)
				end while

				$tile_count_2 := 0
				while($tile_count_2 < $AC_NUM_GROUPS)
					%Ac_Group_PURGE_State[$tile_count_2] := %user_snd_preset_Ac_Group_PURGE[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $AC_NUM_GROUPS) + $tile_count_2]
					inc($tile_count_2)
				end while

				$tile_count_2 := 0
				while($tile_count_2 < $EL_NUM_GROUPS)
					%El_Group_PURGE_State[$tile_count_2] := %user_snd_preset_El_Group_PURGE[(($active_preset - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $EL_NUM_GROUPS) + $tile_count_2]
					inc($tile_count_2)
				end while

				inc($tile_count)
			end while
		end if

		call reset_instrument
		
		fade_in($ALL_EVENTS,2500)
	end function

	{Sound Preset MENU Callback}
		on ui_control ($fact_sound_preset_menu_1)
			if($safe_flag_3 = 1)
				$safe_flag_3 := 0
				call load_sound_preset
				$preset_change_flag := 0
				$safe_flag_3 := 1
			else

			end if

    			if (pgs_get_key_val(PURGE_MODE, 0) = 1)	
	    			$group_count := 0
	    		    while ($group_count < $AC_NUM_GROUPS)
	    		        purge_group($group_count, %Ac_Group_PURGE_State[$group_count])
	    		        inc($group_count)
	    		    end while
    		    	$group_count := 0
    		        while ($group_count < $EL_NUM_GROUPS)
    		            purge_group($group_count + $AC_NUM_GROUPS, %El_Group_PURGE_State[$group_count])
    		            inc($group_count)
    		        end while
	    		end if
	    	end if
		end on

						set_menu_item_str(%sound_preset_controls[06],$active_preset_helper - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS, !user_sound_preset_names[($active_preset_helper - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS)])

						%user_snd_preset_reverb[(($active_preset_helper - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_CONTROLS_REVERB)]		:= %user_snd_preset_reverb[((($active_preset_helper - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) + 1) * $NUM_CONTROLS_REVERB)]
						%user_snd_preset_reverb[(($active_preset_helper - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) * $NUM_CONTROLS_REVERB) + 1]	:= %user_snd_preset_reverb[((($active_preset_helper - $MAX_SOUND_FACT_PRESETS) + 1) * $NUM_CONTROLS_REVERB) + 1]
						
						$arr_count_2 := 0
						while($arr_count_2 < $NUM_USER_SOUND_PRESETS)
							if ($arr_count_2 < %user_num_snd_Presets[0])
								set_menu_item_visibility(%sound_preset_controls[06], $arr_count_2, 1)
							else
								set_menu_item_visibility(%sound_preset_controls[06], $arr_count_2, 0)
							end if
							inc($arr_count_2)
						end while
						inc($active_preset_helper)
					end while
					
				end if

				%save_preset_async_id[00] := save_array(%user_snd_preset_pan, 1)
				while(%save_preset_async_id[00] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while
				%save_preset_async_id[01] := save_array(%user_snd_preset_vol, 1)
				while(%save_preset_async_id[01] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while
				%save_preset_async_id[02] := save_array(%user_snd_preset_solo, 1)
				while(%save_preset_async_id[02] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while
				%save_preset_async_id[03] := save_array(%user_snd_preset_mute, 1)
				while(%save_preset_async_id[03] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while
				%save_preset_async_id[04] := save_array(%user_snd_preset_src_data, 1)
				while(%save_preset_async_id[04] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while
				%save_preset_async_id[05] := save_array(%user_snd_preset_fx_data, 1)
				while(%save_preset_async_id[05] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while
				%save_preset_async_id[06] := save_array(%user_snd_preset_fx_onoff, 1)
				while(%save_preset_async_id[06] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while
				%save_preset_async_id[07] := save_array(%user_snd_preset_master_fx, 1)
				while(%save_preset_async_id[07] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while
				%save_preset_async_id[08] := save_array(%user_snd_preset_master_fx_onoff, 1)
				while(%save_preset_async_id[08] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while
				%save_preset_async_id[09] := save_array(%user_snd_preset_Ac_Selection, 1)
				while(%save_preset_async_id[09] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while
				%save_preset_async_id[10] := save_array(%user_snd_preset_El_Selection, 1)
				while(%save_preset_async_id[10] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while
				%save_preset_async_id[11] := save_array(%user_snd_preset_Ac_Group_PURGE, 1)
				while(%save_preset_async_id[11] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while
				%save_preset_async_id[12] := save_array(%user_snd_preset_El_Group_PURGE, 1)
				while(%save_preset_async_id[12] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while
				%save_preset_async_id[13] := save_array(%user_snd_preset_reverb, 1)
				while(%save_preset_async_id[13] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while
				%save_preset_async_id[14] := save_array(%user_num_snd_Presets, 1)
				while(%save_preset_async_id[14] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while
				%save_preset_async_id[15] := save_array(!user_sound_preset_names, 1)
				while(%save_preset_async_id[15] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while
				
				{while(%save_preset_async_id[00] # -1 or %save_preset_async_id[01] # -1 or %save_preset_async_id[02] # -1 or %save_preset_async_id[03] # -1 or ...
					  %save_preset_async_id[04] # -1 or %save_preset_async_id[05] # -1 or %save_preset_async_id[06] # -1 or %save_preset_async_id[07] # -1 or ...
					  %save_preset_async_id[08] # -1 or %save_preset_async_id[09] # -1 or %save_preset_async_id[10] # -1 or %save_preset_async_id[11] # -1 or ...
					  %save_preset_async_id[12] # -1 or %save_preset_async_id[13] # -1 or %save_preset_async_id[14] # -1 or %save_preset_async_id[15] # -1)
					wait(200)
				end while}

				call load_sound_preset

				$sound_preset_flag := 1

				pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND,0, -1)
				pgs_set_key_val(PRESET_DATA, 0, 0)
				pgs_set_key_val(PRESET_DATA, 1, $sound_preset_flag)
				pgs_set_key_val(PRESET_DATA, 2, $last_sound_preset)
				pgs_set_key_val(PRESET_DATA, 3, 0)
				pgs_set_key_val(PRESET_DATA, 4, 1)
				pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND,0, 1)

				fade_in($ALL_EVENTS,5000)
				$safe_flag_1 := 1
			end if
			if (pgs_key_exists(PURGE_MODE))	
    			if (pgs_get_key_val(PURGE_MODE, 0) = 1)	
	    			$group_count := 0
	    		    while ($group_count < $AC_NUM_GROUPS)
	    		        purge_group($group_count, %Ac_Group_PURGE_State[$group_count])
	    		        inc($group_count)
	    		    end while
    		    	$group_count := 0
    		        while ($group_count < $EL_NUM_GROUPS)
    		            purge_group($group_count + $AC_NUM_GROUPS, %El_Group_PURGE_State[$group_count])
    		            inc($group_count)
    		        end while
	    		end if
	    	end if
		end on

	{CATEGORY MENU Callback}
		on ui_control ($category_mnu)
			$Preset_Category := $category_mnu
			set_control_par(%category_controls_id[01],$CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE,$category_mnu)
			if($safe_flag_3 = 1)
				$safe_flag_3 := 0
				call update_sound_preset_menu
				call load_sound_preset
				$preset_change_flag := 0
				$safe_flag_3 := 1
			end if
			
			pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, -1)
				pgs_set_key_val(PRESET_DATA, 0, 1)
				pgs_set_key_val(PRESET_DATA, 1, 0)
				pgs_set_key_val(PRESET_DATA, 2, $last_sound_preset)
				pgs_set_key_val(PRESET_DATA, 4, 0)
				pgs_set_key_val(PRESET_DATA, 5, $Preset_Category)
			pgs_set_key_val(COMMAND, 0, 1)
			
			if (pgs_key_exists(PURGE_MODE))	
				if (pgs_get_key_val(PURGE_MODE, 0) = 1)	
	    			$group_count := 0
	    		    while ($group_count < $AC_NUM_GROUPS)
	    		        purge_group($group_count, %Ac_Group_PURGE_State[$group_count])
	    		        inc($group_count)
	    		    end while
			    	$group_count := 0
			        while ($group_count < $EL_NUM_GROUPS)
			            purge_group($group_count + $AC_NUM_GROUPS, %El_Group_PURGE_State[$group_count])
			            inc($group_count)
			        end while
	    		end if
	    	end if
		end on

on listener
	select ($NI_SIGNAL_TYPE)
		case $NI_SIGNAL_TIMER_MS
		if ($gui_update = 0)
			$gui_update := 1
			call tile_Select
			call update_sound_preset_menu
			$disp_tile_count := 0
			while ($disp_tile_count < $NUM_TILES)
				{$fx_pointer := $disp_tile_count}
				if (%Tile_has_Mixer[$disp_tile_count] = $YES)
					if ($disp_tile_count = $TILE_MASTER)
						set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$MAST_TRANS_ATTACK], $CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_TR_ATTACK,-1,$TRANS1_SLOT, 1) & " %")
						set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$MAST_TRANS_RELEASE],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_TR_SUSTAIN,-1,$TRANS1_SLOT, 1) & " %")
						set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$MAST_COMP_THRES],   $CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SCOMP_THRESHOLD,-1,$COMP_SLOT, 1) & " dB")
						set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$MAST_COMP_ATTACK],  $CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SCOMP_ATTACK,-1,$COMP_SLOT, 1) & " ms")
						set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$MAST_COMP_RATIO],   $CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SCOMP_RATIO,-1,$COMP_SLOT, 1) & "")
						set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$MAST_COMP_MAKEUP],  $CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SCOMP_MAKEUP,-1,$COMP_SLOT, 1) & " dB")
						set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$MAST_SAT_GAIN],     $CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SHAPE,-1,$SAT_SLOT, 1) & " %")
						set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$MAST_SAT_LEVEL],    $CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,-1,$SAT_SLOT, 1) & " dB")
						set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$MAST_EQ_LOW_FREQ],  $CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_LF_FREQ,-1,$EQ1_SLOT, 1) & " Hz")
						set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$MAST_EQ_LOW_GAIN],  $CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_LF_GAIN,-1,$EQ1_SLOT, 1) & " dB")
						set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$MAST_EQ_MID_FREQ],  $CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_HMF_FREQ,-1,$EQ1_SLOT, 1) & " Hz")
						set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$MAST_EQ_MID_GAIN],  $CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_HMF_GAIN,-1,$EQ1_SLOT, 1) & " dB")
						set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$MAST_EQ_HI_FREQ],   $CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_HF_FREQ,-1,$EQ1_SLOT, 1) & " Hz")
						set_control_par_str (%mast_effects_control_id[$MAST_EQ_HI_GAIN],   $CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SEQ_HF_GAIN,-1,$EQ1_SLOT, 1) & " dB")
						$vol_pointer := $disp_tile_count
						set_control_par_str(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,1) & " dB")
						$pan_pointer  := $disp_tile_count
						set_control_par_str(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_STEREO,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,1))
						if ( $pan_MASTER = 1000000)
							set_control_par_str(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, "Stereo")
						end if
					else
						if ($disp_tile_count = $TILE_REV)
							{$solo_pointer := $disp_tile_count
							call tile_SOLO
							$mute_pointer := $disp_tile_count
							call tile_MUTE}
							$vol_pointer := $disp_tile_count
							set_control_par_str(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SEND_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,-1,$REVERB_SLOT,0) & " dB")
						else 	
							{all OTHER Tiles}
							$vol_pointer  := $disp_tile_count
							set_control_par_str(%volfader_id[$vol_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_INSERT_EFFECT_OUTPUT_GAIN,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$vol_pointer]) & " dB")
							
							$pan_pointer  := $disp_tile_count
							if ($pan_pointer = $TILE_OHS or $pan_pointer = $TILE_OHM or $pan_pointer = $TILE_ROOM)
								if(%oh_stereo[$pan_pointer] # -1)
									if(%oh_stereo[$pan_pointer] = 1)
										{width}
										set_control_par_str(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_STEREO, -1, $SPREAD_SLOT, $NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$pan_pointer]))
										if ( $pan_OHS = 1000000)
											set_control_par_str(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, "Stereo")
										end if
									else
										{pan}
										set_control_par_str(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_STEREO_PAN,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$pan_pointer]))
									end if
								end if
							else
								set_control_par_str(%pan_id[$pan_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL,get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_STEREO_PAN,-1,$SPREAD_SLOT,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$pan_pointer]))
							end if
							{$solo_pointer := $disp_tile_count
							call tile_SOLO}
							$mute_pointer := $disp_tile_count
							{call tile_MUTE}
							set_control_par(%mute_id[$mute_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE,get_control_par(%mute_id[$mute_pointer],$CONTROL_PAR_VALUE))
							{reverb_send}
							set_control_par_str (%effects_control_id[$RVB_SEND],$CONTROL_PAR_LABEL, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_SENDLEVEL_0,-1,$SEND_SLOT,$NI_BUS_OFFSET + %Tile_to_Bus[$disp_tile_count]) & " dB")
						end if
					end if
				end if
				inc($disp_tile_count)
			end while
			change_listener_par($NI_SIGNAL_TIMER_MS,0)
		end if
	end select
end on

on async_complete
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = $load_ir_id)
		$load_ir_id := -1
	end if

	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %save_preset_async_id[00])
		%save_preset_async_id[00] := -1
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %save_preset_async_id[01])
		%save_preset_async_id[01] := -1
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %save_preset_async_id[02])
		%save_preset_async_id[02] := -1
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %save_preset_async_id[03])
		%save_preset_async_id[03] := -1
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %save_preset_async_id[04])
		%save_preset_async_id[04] := -1
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %save_preset_async_id[05])
		%save_preset_async_id[05] := -1
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %save_preset_async_id[06])
		%save_preset_async_id[06] := -1
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %save_preset_async_id[07])
		%save_preset_async_id[07] := -1
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %save_preset_async_id[08])
		%save_preset_async_id[08] := -1
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %save_preset_async_id[09])
		%save_preset_async_id[09] := -1
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %save_preset_async_id[10])
		%save_preset_async_id[10] := -1
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %save_preset_async_id[11])
		%save_preset_async_id[11] := -1
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %save_preset_async_id[12])
		%save_preset_async_id[12] := -1
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %save_preset_async_id[13])
		%save_preset_async_id[13] := -1
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %save_preset_async_id[14])
		%save_preset_async_id[14] := -1
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %save_preset_async_id[15])
		%save_preset_async_id[15] := -1
	end if

	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %load_check_id[00])
		if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS # 1)
			while($init_flag = 1)
				wait(75)
			end while
		end if
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %load_check_id[01])
		if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS # 1)
			while($init_flag = 1)
				wait(75)
			end while
		end if
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %load_check_id[02])
		if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS # 1)
			while($init_flag = 1)
				wait(75)
			end while
		end if
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %load_check_id[03])
		if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS # 1)
			while($init_flag = 1)
				wait(75)
			end while
		end if
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %load_check_id[04])
		if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS # 1)
			while($init_flag = 1)
				wait(75)
			end while
		end if
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %load_check_id[05])
		if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS # 1)
			while($init_flag = 1)
				wait(75)
			end while
		end if
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %load_check_id[06])
		if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS # 1)
			while($init_flag = 1)
				wait(75)
			end while
		end if
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %load_check_id[07])
		if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS # 1)
			while($init_flag = 1)
				wait(75)
			end while
		end if
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %load_check_id[08])
		if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS # 1)
			while($init_flag = 1)
				wait(75)
			end while
		end if
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %load_check_id[09])
		if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS # 1)
			while($init_flag = 1)
				wait(75)
			end while
		end if
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %load_check_id[10])
		if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS # 1)
			while($init_flag = 1)

			end while
		end if
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %load_check_id[11])
		if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS # 1)
			while($init_flag = 1)
				wait(75)
			end while
		end if
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %load_check_id[12])
		if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS # 1)
			while($init_flag = 1)
				wait(75)
			end while
		end if
	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %load_check_id[13])
		if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS # 1)
			while($init_flag = 1)
				wait(75)
			end while

	end if
	if ($NI_ASYNC_ID = %load_check_id[14])
		if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS # 1)
			%user_num_snd_Presets[0] := 0
			$arr_count_1 := 0
			while($arr_count_1 < $NUM_USER_SOUND_PRESETS)
				set_menu_item_visibility(%sound_preset_controls[06], $arr_count_1, 0)
				inc($arr_count_1)
			end while

			@fact_sound_preset_name_1 := get_menu_item_str(%sound_preset_controls[00],$fact_sound_preset_menu_1)
			$active_preset := $fact_sound_preset_menu_1
			@fact_sound_preset_name_2 := get_menu_item_str(%sound_preset_controls[01],$fact_sound_preset_menu_2 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_1)
			$active_preset := $fact_sound_preset_menu_2
			@fact_sound_preset_name_3 := get_menu_item_str(%sound_preset_controls[02],$fact_sound_preset_menu_3 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_1 - $NUM_FACT_SOUND_PRESETS_2)
			$active_preset := $fact_sound_preset_menu_3
